> #cc_videos_00000000316
which is vital to modern experiments in manipulating new potential energy sources.
这对于操纵新型潜在能源的现代实验至关重要。

> #cc_videos_00000000210
With further research and development, uses for this technology would include heavy lifting and the ability to create tractor beams,
随着进一步的研发，这项技术的用途将包括重物吊运和制造牵引光束的能力，

> #cc_videos_00000000211
thereby making low-gravity docking procedures much safer for pilots.
从而使低重力对接程序对飞行员来说更加安全。

> #cc_videos_00000000212
For more information, contact the UAC's Advanced Tool Department.
欲了解更多信息，请联系UAC的高级工具部门。

> #cc_videos_00000000213
Welcome to a new, safer Mars.
欢迎来到一个更安全的新火星。

> #cc_videos_00000000214
This briefing is designed to inform all personnel of our mission goals
本次简报旨在告知所有人员我们的任务目标，

> #cc_videos_00000000317
and act as a reminder of our ongoing commitment to the safety of the entire UAC family.
并提醒我们对整个UAC大家庭安全的持续承诺。

> #cc_videos_00000000215
There are many reasons to be excited about this new UAC Mars mission.
有许多理由对这次新的UAC火星任务感到兴奋。

> #cc_videos_00000000318
Not only will you be part of what promises to be exciting discoveries, you are also laying the groundwork for the future of the UAC.
您不仅将参与到有望带来激动人心发现的工作中，还在为UAC的未来奠定基础。

> #cc_videos_00000000216
We ask for your cooperation in following all UAC procedures outlined in your team manual.
我们请求您配合遵守团队手册中列出的所有UAC规程。

> #cc_videos_00000000319
Discuss any issues or problems with team leaders only. And for your safety, please stay in your team-designated areas.
只与团队负责人讨论任何问题。为了您的安全，请留在团队指定区域。

> #cc_videos_00000000217
Our continuing commitment to safety includes advanced training for all of our security detail.
我们对安全的持续承诺包括为所有安保人员提供高级培训。

> #cc_videos_00000000320
Our security team ratio has been doubled from our last Mars mission to provide our workers
我们的安保团队比例已比上次火星任务增加一倍，旨在为我们的员工提供

> #cc_videos_00000000218
with the absolute safest working conditions.
绝对安全的工作条件。

> #cc_videos_00000000321
The UAC knows that safe workers are happy workers, and we will continue to do everything in our power to provide a secure workplace.
UAC深知安全工作的员工是快乐的员工，我们将继续竭尽所能提供一个安全的工作场所。

> #cc_videos_00000000219
Thank you for your attention and enjoy your stay on Mars.
感谢您的关注，祝您在火星逗留愉快。

> #cc_videos_00000000220
My name is Dr. Richard Meyers, and I'm a research specialist stationed at Exis Labs.
我叫理查德·迈耶斯博士，是艾克西斯实验室的一名研究专家。

> #cc_videos_00000000221
I don't know who will be hearing this, but I wanted to alert someone of the disaster at Mars City.
我不知道谁会听到这段录音，但我希望能提醒某人火星城发生的灾难。

> #cc_videos_00000000322
What has been unleashed across this base is an unimaginable evil, and we only have a slight chance of stopping it.
在这座基地中被释放的是一种无法想象的邪恶，我们只有微乎其微的机会阻止它。

> #cc_videos_00000000222
The research I participated in was the next step in teleportation.
我参与的研究是传送技术发展的下一步。

> #cc_videos_00000000223
To give context to my research, back in 2115, UAC researchers discovered an ancient Martian civilization.
为了说明我的研究背景，早在2115年，UAC的研究员们发现了一个古老的火星文明。

> #cc_videos_00000000323
At the Erebus Dig site, they found a Martian teleportation device.
在厄瑞玻斯挖掘场，他们发现了一个火星传送装置。

> #cc_videos_00000000224
It was non-functional, and all attempts to start it proved fruitless.
它无法运作，所有启动它的尝试都徒劳无功。

> #cc_videos_00000000324
It took many years, but the researchers managed to learn enough from the device and other wall carvings to reverse-engineer it.
这花费了许多年，但研究员们设法从该装置和其它墙壁雕刻中获得了足够的信息，从而对其进行了逆向工程。

> #cc_videos_00000000225
The first prototype teleporter, codenamed Project Mercury, was built in Delta Labs and became operational in 2139.
第一个原型传送器，代号“水星计划”，在德尔塔实验室建造，并于2139年投入运行。

> #cc_videos_00000000226
This teleporter was only capable of short-distance travel and limited quantities of matter transference.
这个传送器只能进行短距离传送和有限的物质传输。

> #cc_videos_00000000227
It could only teleport a single test subject, small animals and chimps usually, across a room.
它只能将单个测试对象，通常是小型动物和黑猩猩，传送到一个房间的距离。

> #cc_videos_00000000228
Once testing intensified and technical data increased, we were able to fabricate more powerful teleporters.
随着测试的加剧和技术数据的增加，我们得以制造出更强大的传送器。

> #cc_videos_00000000229
In Delta Labs, Sector 3, Project Gemini managed to increase teleportation across greater distances.
在德尔塔实验室3区，“双子座计划”成功实现了更远距离的传送。

> #cc_videos_00000000230
In addition to the increased range, we found we could begin transporting human-sized subjects.
除了增加范围，我们还发现可以开始传送人类大小的物体。

> #cc_videos_00000000231
It was during this stage we began to see the effects of opening up these portals to that strange dimension.
正是在这个阶段，我们开始看到打开通往那个陌生维度的传送门所带来的影响。

> #cc_videos_00000000325
Our scientific curiosity overruled the obvious warnings,
我们的科学好奇心压倒了显而易见的警告，

> #cc_videos_00000000232
and under Dr. Malcolm Betruger's direction, we continued experimenting.
在马尔科姆·贝特鲁格博士的指导下，我们继续进行实验。

> #cc_videos_00000000233
On Project Apollo, the engineers developed a room-sized teleporter in Delta Lab Sector 4.
在“阿波罗计划”中，工程师们在德尔塔实验室4区开发了一个房间大小的传送器。

> #cc_videos_00000000234
It was capable of teleporting a small-sized team to destinations on this new, dimensional plane.
它能够将一个小型团队传送到这个新的维度平面上的目的地。

> #cc_videos_00000000235
The expedition teams began exploring and setting up small research outposts.
探险队开始探索并建立小型研究前哨。

> #cc_videos_00000000326
We could only teleport small equipment with the Delta 4 teleporter, and this condition frustrated Dr. Betruger.
我们只能用德尔塔4号传送器传送小型设备，这种情况让贝特鲁格博士感到沮丧。

> #cc_videos_00000000236
Soon after the success of Project Apollo, plans were drawn and work executed on a new facility, Exis Labs.
在“阿波罗计划”成功后不久，便制定了计划并开始建设一个新设施——艾克西斯实验室。

> #cc_videos_00000000237
At Exis Labs, the goal was to create a large teleporter, similar in scale to the one at Erebus.
在艾克西斯实验室，目标是建造一个大型传送器，其规模与厄瑞玻斯那个相似。

> #cc_videos_00000000238
It would be powerful enough to transport large equipment, even dropships, and eventually shorten interstellar travel.
它将强大到足以运输大型设备，甚至空投船，并最终缩短星际旅行时间。

> #cc_videos_00000000239
Betruger was so impatient on seeing results from this research, he had the engineers start work on the teleporter once the facility reached 75% completion.
贝特鲁格对这项研究的结果如此不耐烦，以至于设施达到75%完工时，他就让工程师们开始建造传送器。

> #cc_videos_00000000240
We had expedition teams set up a teleporter outpost in the other dimension to link up with Exis.
我们让探险队在另一个维度建立了一个传送前哨，以便与艾克西斯连接。

> #cc_videos_00000000327
It was at this time I began investigating the strange stories I heard over at Delta Labs.
正是在这个时候，我开始调查我在德尔塔实验室听到的那些奇怪的故事。

> #cc_videos_00000000241
I managed to hack undetected into Betruger's personal logs, and what I found scared me to the core.
我设法在未被察觉的情况下入侵了贝特鲁格的个人日志，我发现的内容让我心惊胆战。

> #cc_videos_00000000328
Betruger became obsessed with the findings of this new dimension.
贝特鲁格开始痴迷于这个新维度的发现。

> #cc_videos_00000000242
He started to push experiments, regardless of the human cost.
他开始不顾人员代价地推进实验。

> #cc_videos_00000000332
His log entries into the occult and how to harness evil powers were truly frightening.
他日志中关于神秘学以及如何驾驭邪恶力量的记录，着实令人恐惧。

> #cc_videos_00000000243
The more recent logs detailed how demons, yes, demons, contacted him through his dreams, offering him unimaginable powers.
最近的日志详细描述了恶魔，是的，就是恶魔，如何通过他的梦境联系他，并向他提供无法想象的力量。

> #cc_videos_00000000244
But they demanded he find a way to help them reclaim Earth. It was then I realized that this other dimension was Hell itself.
但他们要求他找到帮助他们夺回地球的方法。正是在那时我意识到，这个维度就是地狱本身。

> #cc_videos_00000000329
By the time I realized his plan, Betruger had started the invasion.
当我意识到他的计划时，贝特鲁格已经开始了入侵。

> #cc_videos_00000000245
Since the Exis teleporter hadn't reached sufficient functionality, I assumed Betruger decided to launch the demon invasion on Mars without it.
由于艾克西斯传送器尚未达到足够的功能，我猜贝特鲁格决定在没有它的情况下在火星上发动恶魔入侵。

> #cc_videos_00000000246
However, the Hell outpost teleporter is operationally ready, and it's only a matter of time before Betruger decides to use it.
然而，地狱前哨传送器已准备好运行，贝特鲁格决定使用它只是时间问题。

> #cc_videos_00000000247
I'm going to try to reach Chief Engineer Rhodes in the Enpro facility to divert enough power to Exis,
我将尝试联系恩普罗设施的总工程师罗兹，以将足够的电力转移到艾克西斯，

> #cc_videos_00000000330
and with a little luck, create a big enough power surge to destroy it from here.
如果运气好的话，制造足够大的电涌从这里摧毁它。

> #cc_videos_00000000248
I can only pray God will forgive me for my part in all this and help me make things right.
我只能祈求上帝原谅我在这件事中的参与，并帮助我纠正错误。

> #cc_videos_00000000249
Lord save my soul. Richard Meyers, signing off.
主啊，拯救我的灵魂。理查德·迈耶斯，记录结束。
